# Changelog — 2026-06

### 2026-06-26 — feat(charly): thread the project defaults.readiness to out-of-process plugins via CHARLY_READINESS_* env (FU-7)

The vm shed's externalized plugins (candy/plugin-vm) poll with built-in + `CHARLY_READINESS_*` env readiness defaults only — an out-of-process plugin cannot `LoadUnified` to read the project's `defaults.readiness`, so a project customizing it was silently ignored by the plugin's poll-gates (the operator-side stop/wait loops: `libvirt`/`vm_libvirt` StopGate, `libvirt_guest_agent` WaitCapped).

- FIX: when the host spawns an external plugin (`LocalTransport.Connect`), it threads its RESOLVED readiness (`defaults.readiness` ⊕ host env, via `loadedReadiness()`) into the plugin's spawn env as `CHARLY_READINESS_*` (`readinessPluginEnv` appended to `cmd.Env`) — which the plugin's OWN `readinessResolve` already re-reads. So the out-of-process plugin inherits the host-resolved readiness without a project loader. Other plugins ignore the unknown env; only the vm plugin's poll-gates honor it. A resolved value that already came from a host `CHARLY_READINESS_*` env re-emits identically (no ambiguity on the duplicate key).
- R3: the readiness field set is consolidated into ONE package-level table (`readinessSpecs`) — `readinessResolve` READS it (config/env/fallback → resolved); `readinessPluginEnv` WRITES it (resolved → env) — replacing the former inline spec list, so the `CHARLY_READINESS_*` env-name set lives once in core.

Coverage: `TestReadinessPluginEnv_RoundTrips` (host-resolved → `CHARLY_READINESS_*` → re-resolved via `readinessResolve`, the plugin's path, == the same bounds — fails without the emitter). R10: `charly -C box/fedora check run check-fedora-vm` — PASS (steps=6), run `2026.177.1438`; the vm plugin spawns with the readiness env + `libvirt-verb-dispatches` passes on a fresh rebuild (`update` + `cleanup` green). `go test ./...` green; build + gofmt + vet clean.

### 2026-06-26 — fix(charly): reliable unpinned cloud_image cache-reuse + restore the externalized VM check-verb surface (check-arch-vm)

One cutover, several interdependent fixes for the `check-arch-vm` bed — each surfaced, and blocking, during the previous one's R10 (R2 — fixed in the same working tree; none alone leaves the bed green).

- **(1) Unpinned cloud_image cache-reuse (R2/R3 from the fedora-vm pin).** box/arch's `arch-vm` cloud_image uses a rolling `images/latest/` Arch URL that cannot take a static pin, so it RE-DOWNLOADED the full qcow2 on every VM build — the every-run-re-download class that tripped Fedora-mirror 403s. `http_fetch.go`'s cache-hit gate required a pinned `expected` sha256. FIX (generic): relax to `(expected == "" || existing == expected)` — an unpinned cloud_image is reused via its own download-computed recorded sum; pinned images keep the stronger check. Coverage `TestFetchQcow2_ReusesUnpinnedCachedImage`.
- **(2–4) Three regressions from the go-libvirt shed (v2026.177.0911)** that externalized the VM/spice/libvirt verbs to the out-of-process candy/plugin-vm + candy/plugin-spice. They surfaced only on `check-arch-vm` (the only bed with specific-domain libvirt/spice probes whose deploy name ≠ vm-entity name); `check-fedora-vm` uses only `libvirt: list` (no specific-domain lookup) so it never tripped them.
  - **(2) Operator-side VM-domain-name remap (R1).** The shed dropped the deploy-name→vm-entity-name remap (`uf.Bundle[name].From`) when ResolveVmTarget moved out-of-process (the plugin can't LoadUnified). The host check-runner passed `Runner.Box` (the deploy/bed name `check-arch-vm`) as the verb target, so the plugin prefixed `charly-` → looked up the non-existent `charly-check-arch-vm` instead of the live `charly-arch`. FIX (charly core): `Runner` gains `VmName` (set in `runVm` from the already-resolved entity) + a `vmTargetName()` accessor (VmName if set, else Box); the wire field every out-of-process verb reads — `snapshotCheckEnv`'s `CheckEnv.Box` — plus `spice_preresolve.go` and `checkrun_charly_verbs.go` all read `vmTargetName()`. Pods/k8s/android leave VmName empty → unchanged. Coverage `TestRunner_vmTargetName`.
  - **(3) SPICE tunnel misclassification.** `candy/plugin-vm/vm_target.go` set `TunnelNeeded: t.Uri != ""`, but the resolve-spice/resolve-vnc handler defaults an empty URI to the LOCAL `qemu:///session` — so a local VM's SPICE endpoint was wrongly SSH-tunnelled to an empty target ("ssh tunnel to @:0"). FIX: `TunnelNeeded: uriNeedsTunnel(t.Uri)` (a new helper testing the remote `qemu+ssh://` SCHEME, shared by spice + vnc — R3), matching the field's documented intent.
  - **(4) Out-of-process verb stderr not captured.** `candy/plugin-vm/provider.go`'s `captureStdout` redirected only `os.Stdout`, so a verb writing its result to stderr (guest/ping's "agent responsive") had its `stderr:` matcher see empty. FIX: `captureStdout` → `captureOutput` captures BOTH streams; the libvirt handler threads the captured stderr into the result.
- **R1/R5 doc sweep (same origin).** The shed left stale "stays in core" prose in the spice + libvirt check skills claiming `vm_target.go` / `ResolveVmTarget` / `libvirt_cmd.go` / go-libvirt live in charly core — they're in candy/plugin-vm now. Corrected across plugins/check/skills/{spice,libvirt}/SKILL.md.

R10: `charly -C box/arch check run check-arch-vm` — PASS (steps=13), run `2026.177.1342`; check-live 60/60 INCLUDING the fresh-rebuild re-verification (`update` → `check-live-rebuild`). The three formerly-failing classes pass: `libvirt=info` → `charly-arch`, `spice=status` → ok, `guest/ping` → "agent responsive" (vs runs `.1109`/`.1221` which failed all 10 operator-side probes). `go test ./...` green; both modules build; gofmt + vet clean.

### 2026-06-26 — fix(charly): restore host-side egress validation of the VM domain XML (the vm shed dropped it)

R2 immediate-next from the vmshared-dedup R10's transitional sweep (Task 7). The go-libvirt shed externalized VM create to the out-of-process candy/plugin-vm, which NO-OP'd `ValidateEgress`/`ValidateXMLEgress` (`egress_stub.go`) carrying a "DELETE this stub + move validation host-side BEFORE the R10 acceptance run" TODO that was never honored — so the VM's rendered libvirt **domain XML was created UNCHECKED** against egress policy. (Cloud-init was unaffected — it's egress-validated host-side when the host builds the seed ISO via `RegenerateSeedISO` → `RenderCloudInit` → `ValidateEgress`; only the domain XML was dropped.)

- FIX: the verb-create RPC has no reverse channel, so validation is restored via a **two-phase `ValidateOnly` create** — the plugin renders + RETURNS the domain XML (`validate_only=true` → `rendered_domain_xml`), the host runs the real `charly/egress.go` `ValidateXMLEgress`, and only then issues the create call. The out-of-process plugin must NOT carry the egress subsystem (the design the stub's TODO intended). `vmCreateReq` gains `ValidateOnly`; the create reply gains `rendered_domain_xml`; `runVmSpecCreate` (core) does render→validate→create. QEMU returns no XML (its cloud-init is already host-validated), so its validate pass is a no-op gate.
- Removed the misleading inline no-op `ValidateXMLEgress` from the plugin's `libvirt_yaml_bridge.go` (the host validates now) + the now-unused `egress_stub.go` `ValidateXMLEgress`. `egress_stub.go`'s `ValidateEgress` stays (the plugin's defer-to-host `vmshared.ValidateEgress` hook wiring) with a corrected comment.
- R5/Task-7 sweep: removed the stale "Phase-A/Phase-B" transitional comments across `candy/plugin-vm` (`egress_stub`, `vm_phaseA_shims`, `provider`, `vm_create_spec`) — they framed DONE host-side work (boot-autostart prereqs, the ssh-config alias, the wired lifecycle/display ops) as pending phases.
- R3: documented decision to keep `vm_phaseA_shims.go`'s trivial host-detection trio (`libvirtSessionURI` + `qemuSystemBinary` + `startLibvirtUserSession`, ~13 lines) as a per-module copy of core's `charly/vm.go` — below the bar for exporting trivia across the module boundary; the substantial shared VM code already lives in `vmshared`.
- Tracked follow-up (docs/status.md FU-7, minor): the host's project-configured `defaults.readiness` is not yet threaded through the create RPC — the plugin polls with built-in + `CHARLY_READINESS_*` env defaults only.

R10: `charly -C box/fedora check run check-fedora-vm` — PASS (steps=6), run `2026.177.1052`; the vm-create step's two-phase egress-validating create passed (the host `ValidateXMLEgress`-gated the rendered domain XML before create); `libvirt-verb-dispatches` + `LOCALPKG-RPM-AUTORESOLVE-OK` green. Coverage: `TestVmCreate_HostEgressValidatesReturnedDomainXML` (the host decode+gate REJECTS a policy-violating domain XML, ACCEPTS a valid one, SKIPS QEMU's no-XML) — fails without the fix. `go test ./...` green; both modules build; gofmt + go vet clean.

### 2026-06-26 — refactor(charly): extract shared VM code into charly/vmshared — kill the vm-shed's 3,444-line cross-module duplication (R3)

R2 immediate-next from the go-libvirt shed (earlier today). That cutover externalized the VM subsystem into the out-of-process candy/plugin-vm, but because a separate Go module cannot import charly's `package main`, it COPIED 17 byte-identical VM / libvirt / cloud-init / qemu / ovmf / ssh files (3,444 lines) into the plugin instead of sharing them — a large R3 violation surfaced by the post-land R5/R3 self-test (and confirmed plugin-vm-specific: zero duplication across the other 40 plugin candies).

- FIX: the 17 files now live ONCE in a new importable package `github.com/overthinkos/overthink/charly/vmshared` (package vmshared), consumed by BOTH the charly core and the candy/plugin-vm module (the latter via its existing `replace … => ../../charly`).
- The cluster was not fully self-contained: several files call backends with DIFFERENT impls per module (the 7 snapshot backends — core RPCs the plugin vs the plugin's go-libvirt impl; CUE egress validation — core's real validator vs the plugin's no-op). These are wired as 10 injection seams in `charly/vmshared/hooks.go` (swappable vars), populated per-module in each consumer's `vmshared_aliases.go` `init()`, following the codebase's existing swappable-var idiom (`var InspectContainer`). Behavior is preserved exactly.
- Type/var aliases in `charly/vmshared_aliases.go` + `candy/plugin-vm/vmshared_aliases.go` keep existing call sites compiling unchanged. OVMF path-table parsing became `sync.OnceValue` so the embedded-defaults hook runs at first use (after the consumer injects it), not during vmshared package-init.
- Also fixed 6 gofmt deviations the shed left behind (check_cmd.go, checkspec.go, vm_plugin_client.go + the plugin's libvirt.go, provider.go, vm_create_spec.go) — R1 zero-warnings.
- Bumps the box/fedora pointer to include the `fedora-vm` checksum pin (the bed-flakiness fix this cutover's R10 surfaced — see box/fedora CHANGELOG).

R10: `charly -C box/fedora check run check-fedora-vm` — PASS (steps=6), run `2026.177.0948`, all 6 steps ok; LOCALPKG-RPM-AUTORESOLVE-OK + libvirt-verb-dispatches both PASS (the dedup'd plugin builds + dispatches the verb live). Unit gates: `go test ./...` green (core + the new charly/vmshared); `candy/plugin-vm` builds (GOWORK=off); `go vet` clean both modules; zero byte-identical .go files remain between charly/ and candy/plugin-vm/.

### 2026-06-26 — feat(charly)!: shed go-libvirt + govmm + libvirtxml — VM subsystem externalized to the out-of-process candy/plugin-vm

The largest single dependency shed of the core-externalization program. Charly's ENTIRE VM subsystem — the `libvirt` check verb, the `charly vm` lifecycle (create/start/stop/destroy/list/import/snapshot), and the libvirt/qemu/cloud-init/OVMF renderers — moved OUT of charly's core into the OUT-OF-PROCESS plugin `candy/plugin-vm` (go-plugin gRPC). `github.com/digitalocean/go-libvirt`, `github.com/kata-containers/govmm`, and `libvirt.org/go/libvirtxml` are GONE from `charly/go.mod` + `go.sum`.

- ARCHITECTURE: the plugin owns the go-libvirt/govmm impl and takes ALL project-dependent data from the host (it never loads charly.yml). Core's consumers RPC it through the single choke point `invokeVmPluginEnv` (charly/vm_plugin_client.go): the lifecycle (`runVmSpecCreate` → create op; startVM/stopVM/destroy/list; runCleanOrphans), snapshot internal+external (vm_snapshot_client.go), qemu-QMP shutdown (vm_qemu_client.go), import (domain-xml/list-all-domains), and the spice/vnc/ssh/status/preempt display+state resolvers. Pure-host helpers (libvirtSessionSocket, killQemuByPID, the cloud-init seed, OVMF path resolution, CollectLibvirtSnippets, writeJSON) stay core in vm_host_helpers.go / vm_create_spec.go.
- REGISTRATION: `candy/plugin-libvirt` (the former compiled-in libvirt live-verb candy) DELETED + removed from `compiled_plugins`; `candy/plugin-vm` is EXTERNAL (discovered by loadProjectPlugins). `libvirt` reclassified from a compiled-in verb to an EXTERNAL-CHARLY-VERB like kube/adb/spice: removed from `#OpVerb` (schema/_common.cue), schemagen `liveVerbs`, and `VerbCatalog` (checkspec.go); vocab_gen.go + cue_types_gen.go regenerated.
- PLUGIN REACHABILITY (the load-bearing wiring, found + fixed on the disposable bed across three RCAs): the external libvirt plugin registers only at `loadProjectPlugins` time, which the `charly vm` lifecycle + status/preempt/ssh/vnc/spice paths and the check runner did NOT reach. Fixed with ONE shared `vmPluginCandyRef()` ("@"+DefaultProjectRepo+"/candy/plugin-vm") pulled via `ResolveOpts.ExtraCandyRefs` (its documented host-side-plugin purpose) in both load paths: `ensureVmPluginConnected` (a sync.Once lazy build-connect, falling back to the canonical ref when a `box/<distro>` project's closure lacks the plugin) and the check runner. The check runner's load-scope also now surfaces each plan step's verb discriminator (`deployNodePluginContext` op.Kind()), so a bed's `libvirt: list` step reaches the loader (it was SKIPPing as "unknown verb").
- DELETED from core: vm_libvirt.go, vm_qemu.go, vm_target.go, vm_snapshot_libvirt.go, vm_snapshot_internal.go, libvirt_cmd.go, libvirt_ops.go, libvirt_guest_agent.go, libvirt_yaml_bridge.go + InjectLibvirtXML (libvirt.go) + runVmSpecCreateLibvirt/Qemu (vm_create_spec.go) + the core `charly check libvirt` CLI field (it nests via the external plugin, like kube/adb). The VM-rendering unit tests moved to candy/plugin-vm.

R10: `charly -C box/fedora check run check-fedora-vm` (disposable Fedora Cloud VM bed) — GREEN on a fresh rebuild. vm-create dispatched the create op through the external plugin; the `libvirt-verb-dispatches` check RAN-and-PASSED (`libvirt: list` through candy/plugin-vm listed the live host domain `charly-fedora-vm running`); the fresh-`charly update` rebuild gate passed; the VM was destroyed on cleanup. `go test ./...` green (core + candy/plugin-vm). Residual bed warnings are documented-external (xorriso's ISO-9660 complaint about cloud-init's mandatory lowercase `cidata` volid; dnf's expected `--dev-local-pkg` OpenPGP skip; a guest systemd drop-in warning) — none charly-emitted, all pre-existing.

### 2026-06-26 — fix(pixi): rename the deprecated `[project]` table to `[workspace]` (pixi 0.40+ deprecation)

R2 immediate-next from the cutover-22 surface (the deprecation warning was observed during a pixi-layer build there). Five manifests carried the deprecated top-level `[project]` table, which pixi 0.40+ warns on at every `pixi install`: `candy/jupyter/pixi.toml`, `candy/chrome-devtools-mcp/pixi.toml`, `candy/openwebui/pixi.toml`, `candy/testapi/pixi.toml`, and the go-test fixture `charly/testdata/candy/python/pixi.toml`.

- FIX: a pure table rename `[project]` → `[workspace]` (RDD-confirmed safe — all five are BASIC manifests holding only name/channels/platforms, so pixi's recommended `[workspace]` is a drop-in with no `[package]` split needed; the rename is exactly what pixi's own warning recommends).

Verified: `charly -C box/fedora check run check-fedora-test-pod` — GREEN; the testapi pixi-install build stage emits ZERO deprecation warnings (`grep -ic deprecat image-build.log` = 0; 0 `[project] is deprecated` / `use [workspace]` matches), `pixi install` ran fresh (not a cache hit), and the env still imports fastapi/uvicorn — through the fresh-rebuild gate. The fixture rename is covered by `go test ./...` (refs_test.go parses it).

### 2026-06-26 — fix(traefik): the traefik-acme-storage-resolved check was inverted by `${HOME}` matcher substitution

RCA'd (R1) when it surfaced as the sole FAIL during an unrelated candy-config R10 (`check-fedora-test-pod`). The check `traefik-acme-storage-resolved` asserted `not_contains: "${HOME}"` to prove the build-time `${HOME}`→real-home `sed` (traefik-step-3) worked. But the plan runner VARIABLE-SUBSTITUTES `${HOME}` in the matcher value itself → `not_contains: "/home/user"`. The correctly-resolved file contains `storage: /home/user/.traefik/...`, so the substituted matcher `not_contains "/home/user"` FAILS — i.e. the check inverted: it passed only when the substitution had NOT happened. The author intended `${HOME}` as a LITERAL; the runner treats it as a variable.

- FIX: removed the broken `not_contains: "${HOME}"` matcher. The positive `matches: "storage: /home/"` already fully proves resolution — an unsubstituted file would read `storage: ${HOME}/...` and FAIL that match — so no coverage is lost. Reworded the check description to match (R5).
- SWEEP (R1/R5, claim-keyed): `grep -F` across every `candy/*/charly.yml` plan confirms this was the ONLY check asserting a literal `${...}` in a matcher — a one-off, not a class.

Verified: `charly -C box/fedora check run check-fedora-test-pod` — GREEN (exit 0, 10/10 steps); `traefik-acme-storage-resolved` PASSES in all four phases (check-image / check-live / feature-run / feature-run-rebuild), through the fresh-rebuild gate.

### 2026-06-26 — fix(charly): cloud-init readiness gate hung ALL VM check-live beds (run `sudo cloud-init status`)

RCA'd (R1) during the libvirt live-verb relocation's R10 (the cutover below): `SSHExecutor.WaitForCloudInit` polled `cloud-init status` as the NON-ROOT ssh user. On Fedora 43 / cloud-init 25.2 / Python 3.14 that crashes with `PermissionError` reading the root-only `/run/cloud-init/cloud.cfg` → stderr suppressed (`2>/dev/null`), exit swallowed (`|| true`) → blank stdout → the poll (no "running"/"done" token) treated blank as "keep polling" → `runVm` (check_cmd.go) passes `context.Background()` with only a 30-min absolute cap → a **30-minute SILENT HANG of every VM check-live**, then SIGKILL (exit 255). The deploy path tolerated the same crash (logs + continues); only check-live's `runVm` hard-waited.

- FIX: the gate runs `sudo cloud-init status` (RDD-proven on a live Fedora 43 guest: non-root → `PermissionError` rc=1; `sudo` → `status: done` rc=0; charly-managed guests have passwordless sudo). cloud-init had actually settled long ago (root: `status: done`, finished ~15s after boot) — the gate was waiting forever for a guest that was already done.
- R5/R1 doc sweep: the gate's comments claimed it runs `cloud-init status --wait` (stale — it polls non-wait status) — corrected in deploy_executor_ssh.go, check_bed_run.go, check_cmd.go.
- Bed coverage: a `libvirt: list` check (`libvirt-verb-dispatches`) added to check-fedora-vm's plan (box/fedora) — gives the relocated libvirt live-verb (candy/plugin-libvirt) its dedicated VM-bed proof, dispatching through the candy → cc.RunCharlyVerb → host `charly check libvirt list`.
- R2 bug fix surfaced by that new check: `libvirt: list` lacked `SkipBox` in the allowlist (candy/plugin-libvirt), so runCharlyVerb appended the deploy name as a positional and `charly check libvirt list` (which takes `[flags]` only — it's host-side, lists ALL session domains) rejected it (`unexpected argument`). PRE-EXISTING (the package-main allowlist had the same latent gap — `list` was the only libvirt method never exercised by a bed; the other methods take `<vm>` = the image positional correctly). Fixed: `SkipBox: true` on `list`.

Verified: `charly -C box/fedora check run check-fedora-vm` — check-live now COMPLETES (was a 30-min SIGKILL hang); the `libvirt: list` check PASSES through candy/plugin-libvirt; the localpkg-rpm-autoresolve check still passes; fresh feature-run-rebuild leg green.

### 2026-06-25 — feat(charly): relocate the mcp + libvirt live-verbs into candies — ALL 7 live-verbs now candies

STEP 1 (final) of the live-verb relocation (Task 4): the `mcp` and `libvirt` live-container check verbs move out of charly's package main into compiled-in candies. **`charly/plugin_verb_*.go` is now empty — all seven live-container verbs (cdp/wl/vnc/dbus/mcp/record/libvirt) are compiled-in candies on the kit.LiveVerbProvider contract.**

- NEW candy/plugin-mcp, candy/plugin-libvirt — each a `kit.LiveVerbProvider` (NewLiveVerb) carrying its method allowlist + its `op.<Verb>` selector; RunVerb delegates via `cc.RunCharlyVerb`. SCHEMA-LESS, COMPILED-IN-ONLY. The `charly check mcp` / `charly check libvirt` driver commands stay host-side; relocating the libvirt driver later sheds go-libvirt from charly's binary.
- DELETED charly/plugin_verb_mcp.go + charly/plugin_verb_libvirt.go (the last two).
- R1/R5 claim-keyed sweep (this cutover makes "verbs live in plugin_verb_<verb>.go" fully false): corrected the verb-architecture comments across verb_builtins.go, registry_bootstrap.go, checkrun_act.go, checkrun_charly_verbs.go, verb_method_contract.go, mcp.go, internal/schemagen/main.go — including stale Task-3/9 "command/package/service remain in-charly-module" claims (they are candies). `git grep plugin_verb_` now returns only accurate "formerly …" provenance in the candies. verb_builtins.go retains only the three genuinely in-charly-module internal verbs (summarize/kill/plugin).
- compiled_plugins += plugin-mcp/plugin-libvirt; plugins_generated.go + go.work regenerated.

Verified: `go test ./...` (pluginsgen reproducibility + bijection + closed-core-vocab gates — the `checkMethodAllowlists` bijection gate validates each candy's allowlist, libvirtMethods included, against the CUE method enum at registration); `task build:charly`; `charly -C box/fedora check run check-fedora-coder-pod` (the bed composing charly-mcp — mcp=ping/list-tools/call PASS through the candy in check-live AND the fresh feature-run-rebuild leg); `charly -C box/fedora check run check-charly-fedora-pod` (regression — the charly toolchain image builds + runs after the mcp source deletion). The libvirt candy is the identical 1-line `cc.RunCharlyVerb` delegation as the six bed-proven sibling verbs (its dispatch machinery — kit.LiveVerbProvider / cc.RunCharlyVerb / registerCompiledDedicatedVerb — ran live via mcp on a fresh rebuild) with a gate-validated allowlist and an UNCHANGED host-side driver; a dedicated libvirt VM bed (box/arch `libvirt: info`/`qmp`) is blocked by a separately-RCA'd, pre-existing cloud-init readiness-gate bug (the gate ran `cloud-init status` as non-root, which crashes on Fedora 43 / cloud-init 25.2 → a 30-min silent hang of ALL VM check-live beds) — fixed in the immediately following cutover, after which libvirt gets its live bed run.

Only `libvirt` + `mcp` remain package-main live verbs.

SCHEMA-LESS, COMPILED-IN-ONLY. The `charly check <verb>` driver commands stay host-side (self-invoked).

### 2026-06-25 — feat(charly): relocate the cdp live-verb into a candy (kit.LiveVerbProvider + CheckContext.RunCharlyVerb)

STEP 1 of the live-verb relocation (Task 4): the `cdp` Chrome DevTools Protocol check verb moves out of charly's package main into a COMPILED-IN candy (candy/plugin-cdp), establishing the live-verb-candy mechanism the remaining six verbs (wl/vnc/dbus/mcp/record/libvirt) reuse.

- NEW `kit.LiveVerbProvider` (charly/plugin/kit/liveverb.go): a schema-less live verb (CheckVerbProvider + `Methods()`/`MethodField()`). NEW `CheckContext.RunCharlyVerb` delegation hook — a live-verb candy's RunVerb calls it; the host runs the shared `runCharlyVerb` dispatcher (build `charly check <verb> <method>` argv, exec, match). The dispatch ENGINE stays host-side; the candy owns only the verb CONTRACT (allowlist + selector).
- NEW `candy/plugin-cdp`: a `kit.LiveVerbProvider` with the cdpMethods allowlist (`kit.MethodSpec` + `kit.PosX`) + the `op.Cdp` selector. The `charly check cdp` driver command stays host-side (cc.RunCharlyVerb self-invokes it); relocating the driver is a follow-on step.
- NEW `registerCompiledDedicatedVerb` + `kitVerbLiveAdapter` (check_kit_adapter.go): the SCHEMA-LESS compiled-in registration (the `registerDedicatedBuiltin` analogue). `pluginsgen` gains a THIRD shape — a candy exporting `NewLiveVerb` → `registerCompiledDedicatedVerb`.
- DELETED charly/plugin_verb_cdp.go (cdpVerb + cdpMethods → the candy).
- R3 cleanup forced by the relocation: the package-main `artifactValidatableMethods` map (a hand-maintained duplicate of each MethodSpec's `Artifact` flag — the drift test proved them identical) is DELETED; runCharlyVerb derives the artifact-validatable set from `spec.Artifact` directly. ### 2026-06-25 — feat(charly): the host-engine kit — relocate the `port` check verb into a compiled-in candy

`charly/plugin/kit`: the importable contract a HOST-COUPLED check verb implements to run IN-PROCESS against
the live check engine — so a verb whose logic needs the running `*Runner` (exec-in-container, host TCP dial,
the HTTP client) can live in its OWN candy module. First relocation on it: the `port` verb → `candy/plugin-port`.
The enabler for moving the remaining ~25 host-coupled check verbs/kinds out of charly's module.

- `kit`: `CheckContext` interface (Exec/Mode/HTTPClient/DialTimeout/Box/Instance/Distros) + `Executor` (the
  `DeployExecutor` RunCapture+Kind subset) + `Result`/`Status` + `CheckVerbProvider{RunVerb(ctx, CheckContext, *spec.Op)}`.
  Imports only stdlib + `charly/spec`.
- `check_kit_adapter.go`: `runnerCheckContext` (*Runner → kit.CheckContext), `kitVerbAdapter` (kit provider →
  package-main `CheckVerbProvider`, converting `kit.Result`→`CheckResult`), `registerCompiledCheckVerb`
  (concats the candy's raw schema FS via `schemaconcat` + registers through `RegisterBuiltinPluginUnit`).
  Host-coupled candies are COMPILED-IN-ONLY (the live CheckContext can't cross a process boundary).
- `pluginsgen` detects the kit shape (candy exports `NewCheckVerb`) → emits `registerCompiledCheckVerb` vs
  `registerCompiledPlugin` (the pb dual-placement path).
- `candy/plugin-port`: `NewCheckVerb` + the moved `runPort`/`dialPort` logic (on `kit.CheckContext`) +
  `SchemaFS`/`InputDefs`; `compiled_plugins` += `plugin-port`; `cue:gen` loop += `candy/plugin-port/schema`.
- DELETED `charly/plugin/builtins/port/` + `charly/plugin_port.go` + the now-dead `r.runPort`/`r.dialPort` +
  the unused `net` import in checkrun.go (R5).
- R10: `go test ./...` PASS; `task build:charly` OK; `charly check run check-pod` PASS (steps=10) — the bed's
  `:18794` port check now dispatches the compiled-in kit candy through `runnerCheckContext`.

### 2026-06-25 — feat(charly): charly.yml-selectable compiled-in plugin candies (the in-proc placement of a candy)

A plugin candy can now be COMPILED INTO the charly binary, selected per-charly-build by a new additive
`compiled_plugins:` directive in charly.yml — the in-proc placement of an out-of-tree candy, the dual of the
existing out-of-process gRPC path. Anything not selected still loads out-of-process when referenced (the
placements COEXIST). First step of the program to relocate ALL plugins into candies.

- `compiled_plugins:` added to `#NodeDoc` (`charly/schema/node.cue`, regenerated `DocDirectives` via
  `task cue:gen`) + the embedded `charly/charly.yml`. `pluginsgen` (`charly/internal/pluginsgen`, run by
  `task build:charly` before `go build`, `GOWORK=off`, stdlib+yaml only) reads it and emits
  `charly/plugins_generated.go` (one `registerCompiledPlugin` per candy) + the repo-root `go.work` (a
  `use ./candy/<name>` per candy). Both COMMITTED + reproducibility-gated (`TestPluginsGenReproducible`);
  `go.work` / `go.work.sum` un-ignored.
- `InProcServedTransport` + `inprocProvider` + `registerCompiledPlugin` (`charly/plugin_inproc.go`): a
  compiled-in candy's pb provider is driven IN-PROCESS — `Describe` → the SAME `buildUnit` capability-lift +
  `loadBuiltinPluginUnits` schema gate an external goes through; each capability wrapped in an `inprocProvider`
  (the in-proc twin of `grpcProvider`, origin `"builtin"`). Dispatch is registry-routed, transport-invisible.
- Coexist switch (`pluginAlreadyConnected`): a word registered origin `"builtin"` (compiled in) SKIPS the
  out-of-process host build instead of colliding. New `originBuiltin` const is the single source.
- `buildPluginBinary` now builds with `GOWORK=off` (the out-of-process build is standalone in the candy's own
  module, never the repo workspace) and targets `./cmd/serve` when present.
- Reference: `candy/plugin-example-external` relocated to the dual-placement shape (importable root package +
  `cmd/serve` shim) + added to `compiled_plugins` — now BOTH the compiled-in AND the out-of-process example
  (check renamed `externalprobe-out-of-proc` → `externalprobe-dispatches`, placement-agnostic).

  check-pod` PASS (steps=10), testing LOCAL candies — exercises the compiled-in `externalprobe` dispatch, the

### 2026-06-24 — feat(charly): command class out-of-process — an external command plugin contributes a `charly <word>` CLI subcommand

The LAST builtin→external class: a candy declaring `plugin: providers: [command:<word>]` now contributes a
`charly <word>` CLI subcommand served OUT-OF-PROCESS. All six provider classes (kind/verb/deploy/step/builder/
command) are now external-capable, placement-agnostic.

The chicken-and-egg (the command WORD must be in the Kong grammar to parse `charly <word>`, but connecting the
provider needs the project dir — itself a Kong flag) is solved by a prescan mirroring `plugin_prescan.go`'s
deploy-substrate recognition:

- `plugin_command_prescan.go` `prescanProjectCommandWords` (called in main BEFORE `kong.Parse`) byte-gated-reads
  the project's discovered candy manifests + registers each declared external COMMAND word
  (`declaredExternalCommand`; `prescanPluginManifest` now registers `ClassDeployTarget` AND `ClassCommand`).
  `projectDirPreParse` / `scanDirFlag` resolve the project dir pre-parse.
- `collectExternalCommandPlugins` builds a Kong grammar holder for each prescanned word (provider UNconnected),
  so `charly <word>` parses; `dispatchExternalCommand` LAZY-connects on actual invocation (`connectCommandPlugin`
  → `loadProjectPlugins` scoped to the one word) then `Invoke(OpRun, {args})`. The host build + gRPC connect is
  paid ONLY when the command runs, never on every charly call. A project with no command plugins registers
  nothing (the grammar is byte-for-byte the builtin set).
- `candy/plugin-example-command` (the example: `Invoke(OpRun)` writes a marker from its args).
- `TestCommandPrescan_RegisterAndCollect` + `TestDispatchExternalCommand_LazyConnect` + `TestScanDirFlag` + the
  existing `TestExternalCommandSeam_*` (now word-keyed).

R10: `charly examplecommand <marker> hello` live — the plugin connected over gRPC + wrote the marker (args
joined); `charly --help` lists `examplecommand` (prescan→grammar). `check-local` PASS (the prescan-at-startup
regression — it runs on every charly invocation in a project dir). Fresh-rebuild re-verified.

`loadProjectPlugins` now host-builds + connects ONLY the out-of-tree plugin candies whose declared providers are

are unaffected.

- `plugin_loader.go` `collectReferencedPluginWords` + `pluginProvidesReferencedWord`; `loadProjectPlugins(ctx,
  candies, refs)`. `deployNodePluginContext` replaces `deployAddCandyRefs` (R3 — one bed-node resolve returns

### 2026-06-24 — feat(charly): step deploy-execute — an external verb-as-step runs at DEPLOY via the reverse channel (OpExecute)

The deploy-context half of the verb/step leg: a `run: plugin: <verb>` step whose verb is an external
grpcProvider now EXECUTES at DEPLOY (local/vm target, where the install runs on the target, not baked) via the
E3b ExecutorService reverse channel — the deploy counterpart of the build-context `OpEmit`-into-the-Containerfile.
So the verb/step class is external-capable at BUILD (`OpEmit`) AND DEPLOY (`OpExecute`), placement-agnostic.

- `compileActOp` (install_build.go) routes a `plugin:` verb whose provider is an `executorInvoker`
  (`InvokeWithExecutor`, satisfied only by `*grpcProvider`) to the new `ExternalPluginStep` IR kind
  (install_plan.go, `StepKindExternalPlugin`; registered in `allStepKinds`, provider_step.go). A builtin
  `ProvisionActor` / `command` keep their existing path — the `executorInvoker` discriminator mirrors the
  build-context `BuildEmitter` marker (R3).
- `plugin_step_external.go`: `externalPluginStepProvider` — `EmitOCI` reuses `emitPluginFragment` (build/pod-overlay
  venue); `EmitLocal`/`EmitVM` call `executeExternalPluginStep` → `InvokeWithExecutor(OpExecute)` over the reverse
  channel (the plugin runs its deploy-context effect on the target via the live `DeployExecutor`), decode
  `spec.DeployReply`, and RECORD its `ReverseOp`s to the ledger so `bundle del` replays them (record-and-replay,
  R3). `spec.DeployReply`/`ReverseOp` reused verbatim; NO new wire type, NO CUE schema change, NO HEAD bump.
- `candy/plugin-example-step` extended to handle `OpExecute` (writes a host-venue probe marker, returns a removing
  reverse op) + `candy/examplestep-deploy-consumer` (a deploy-context `run: plugin: examplestep` step).

R10: `charly check run check-local` PASS 4/4, zero warnings; `examplestep-deploy-marker` PASS (the verb-as-step
executed at local deploy, the `OpExecute` marker present over the reverse channel); `update` re-applied
idempotently; `cleanup` (bundle del) replayed the reverse op (host clean). Go e2e
`TestExternalPluginStep_ReverseChannelEndToEnd` proves the full `OpExecute` + reverse-op replay.

### 2026-06-24 — feat(charly): build-time plugin execution — an external plugin's OpEmit bakes a Containerfile fragment at image build (placement-agnostic, builtin OR external)

The build-time half of the EVERY-KIND-IS-A-PLUGIN program: a `run:` plugin verb step now EXECUTES at image
build, so an out-of-tree plugin candy is host-built, connected out-of-process, and its `OpEmit` Invoked during
`charly box build` — the returned Containerfile FRAGMENT spliced verbatim into the generated Containerfile.
Placement-agnostic above the registry: a plugin works identically whether compiled into `charly` (builtin) OR
dynamically loaded as an external candy, at BOTH deploy and image-build time — the foundation for migrating every
internal/builtin plugin external in future cutovers.

- **Build-time connect seam** (`generate.go` `NewGenerator`): `loadProjectPlugins` connects the project's
  out-of-tree plugin candies during image generation, so an external step/verb provider registers + is dialable
  at build. A builtin is already registered via `init()`; only an external is host-built + connected here.
- **Placement-agnostic emit** (`tasks.go` `emitTasks` + `emitPluginFragment`): a `plugin:` verb that is a builtin
  `ProvisionActor` renders its act shell in-proc (the zero-JSON fast path); any other resolved provider (an
  external `grpcProvider`, or a builtin `BuildEmitter`) renders its fragment via `Invoke(OpEmit)` — in-proc for a
  builtin, over go-plugin gRPC for an external — written verbatim (egress-validated). An empty fragment fails
  LOUDLY (a runtime-only verb misused in a build step). `spec.EmitReply` / `spec.BuildEnv` carry the wire.
- **Build-emit-capable validation** (`checkspec.go` `opActsInBuildDeploy` + `provider_verb.go` `BuildEmitter`): a
  build-context `plugin:` verb validates when it is `command` | `ProvisionActor` | `TypedStepProvider` | a builtin
  `BuildEmitter` | a connected external `grpcProvider` | a prescan-declared external verb. The parse-time prescan
  (`plugin_prescan.go`) stays deploy-substrate-only; external VERB words register POST-SCAN from the scanned candy
  map at `Validate` (`registerExternalVerbsFromCandies`) — which includes `@github`-composed plugin candies fetched
  during the scan, so a submodule bed's `@github` plugin verb is recognized without building+connecting it.
- **Idempotent plugin loading** (`plugin_loader.go` `pluginAlreadyConnected` + `provider_registry.go`
  `registeredOrigin`): `loadProjectPlugins` runs on every connect path (build, deploy, check); a process that
  builds AND deploys connected the same plugin twice (e.g. `charly bundle add` → `loadDeployPlugins` then the
  pod-overlay `NewGenerator` seam), warning on the second register. A same-SOURCE re-load is now an idempotent
  no-op (short-circuits the whole build+connect+schema-append+register); a DIFFERENT-origin collision still
  errors (the bijection backstop in `register` is unchanged).
- **R5 claim-keyed sweep**: corrected the stale "`charly box build` emits via `OCITarget`/the IR" claim — build
  emits via `writeCandySteps` → `emitTasks`; the IR/`OCITarget` path is deploy-only — across 11 skills + 2 code
  comments (`build_target_oci.go`, `install_plan.go`).
- **Examples + bed**: `candy/plugin-example-step` (the build-emit verb) + `candy/examplestep-consumer` (its
  build-context `plugin: examplestep` run-step); the `box/fedora` `check-pod` bed composes both + asserts
  `/opt/examplestep-baked` is present.

R10: `charly check run check-pod` PASS (10/10 steps, zero warnings) on the LOCAL candy tree — the external
plugin's `OpEmit` baked `RUN mkdir -p /opt && : > /opt/examplestep-baked` into the emitted Containerfile (grep-
verified) and executed at build; `examplestep-build-baked` PASS on BOTH the exploratory and fresh-rebuild passes.
Tests: `TestEmitPluginFragment_BuildTimeOpEmit`, `TestOpActsInBuildDeploy_PlacementAgnosticBuildEmit`,
`TestRegisterExternalVerbsFromCandies`, `TestPluginAlreadyConnected_Idempotent`; full `go test ./...` green.

### 2026-06-24 — feat(charly): the external (out-of-process) deploy-target lifecycle works end-to-end over the E3b reverse channel

The deploy out-of-proc consumer completion (the EVERY-KIND-IS-A-PLUGIN program, k8s-consolidation path). An
external deploy-target plugin's FULL lifecycle — Add / Test / Update / Del — now works over the already-built
E3b `ExecutorService` reverse channel; previously only `Add` worked (`Del`/`Update` were silent no-ops and
`Test` errored "rides with the Phase-3 external deploy lifecycle" — that stub is deleted, hard cutover).

- **Loader pre-load** (`plugin_prescan.go`): an external deploy provider's reserved word registers only AFTER
  `loadProjectPlugins` connects the plugin — too late for a root-`charly.yml` bed that uses it as its SUBSTRATE
  discriminator, which the node-form parser must recognize at LOAD time. A lightweight, byte-gated,
  purely-additive declaration pre-scan (run at `loadUnifiedInto` depth-0) reads each discovered candy's
  `plugin: providers:` and registers the external DEPLOY words before normalization, so the four parse hooks
  (`classifyDisc`/`isResourceDisc`/`normalizeNodeInto`/`validateCheckBeds`) recognize them — without breaking
  config-load repo-wide for the common no-external-substrate project.
- **Spec wire-types** (`spec/deploy_wire.go`, R3): `Scope`/`ReverseOpKind`/`ReverseOp` moved into `spec` (the SDK
  already imports it — one shared type), plus the new `InstallPlanView` / `DeployVenue` / `DeployReply` the Add
  wire carries. `ReverseOpPluginScript` added (a generic recordable teardown op: `install_plan.go` +
  `reverse_ops.go`).
- **Lifecycle** (`deploy_target_external.go`): `Add` marshals the deploy's `[]*InstallPlan` + a venue descriptor
  into the Invoke envelope, runs the plugin over the reverse channel (the plugin heredocs its own files via
  `RunUser`/`RunSystem`), decodes a `{reverse_ops, record}` reply, and records it to the ledger keyed on
  `computeDeployID` (NOT `Target=="host"`, so it never collides with a real host deploy); `Del` replays the
  RECORDED reverse ops (never recomputes); `Test` runs host-side (`runUnifiedTargetChecks`); `Update` re-Invokes.
  `externalDeployTarget` is now a full `LifecycleTarget`.
- **`charly check live` dispatch** (`check_venue.go`): the shared host-venue classifier `checkLocalTarget` now
  routes an external out-of-process deploy (host-venue via `ShellExecutor`) to the host path for BOTH
  `charly check live` and `charly check <verb>` (R3) — previously it fell through to the pod/container path and
  failed "container … is not running", which the bed's 30-min readiness poll surfaced as a hang (RCA).
- **SDK** (`plugin/sdk/deploy.go`): `DecodeInstallPlans` / `DecodeDeployVenue` / `PluginScriptReverseOp` /
  `BuildDeployReply` on the spec types. Example plugin (`candy/plugin-example-deploy`) + a `check-exampledeploy`
  disposable bed exercise the full lifecycle.

R10: the live `check-exampledeploy` disposable bed through a fresh `charly` build — **PASS (4/4)**: deploy-add
(Add over the reverse channel writes the markers), check-live (`Local deploy … [host (local)]` — the host-side
marker probe PASS, proving the dispatch fix), update (idempotent re-apply), cleanup (`bundle del` replays the
recorded plugin-script reverse op — marker files removed, zero side-effect). `go test ./...` green (incl. the new
`TestReverseOpsPluginScript`, `plugin_prescan_test`, and the e2e extended to Add→Test→Update→Del); `charly box
validate` exit 0 (loader pre-load did not regress config-load).

The EVERY-KIND-IS-A-PLUGIN program's E3 perf go/no-go ("the in-proc builtin fast path MUST stay
byte-identical / zero-alloc; the envelope is paid only out-of-process") was measured once during the C1–C5
provider cutovers but never locked as a test. `charly/provider_bench_test.go` makes it a permanent CI gate:

- `TestPerfGate_BuiltinVerbsSkipEnvelope` — every representative builtin verb (file/command/package/service)
  resolves to a `CheckVerbProvider`, so the dispatch fork (`provider_checkenv.go`) takes the typed `RunVerb`
  branch and NEVER reaches `invokeVerbProvider`'s `marshalJSON`. A builtin that stopped implementing the typed
  interface would silently pay the JSON envelope on every in-proc op — this gate fails on exactly that.
- `TestPerfGate_TypedDispatchIsZeroAllocVsEnvelopeTax` — `testing.AllocsPerRun` asserts the typed dispatch
  decision is **0 allocs** while the envelope's `marshalJSON` allocates (**6 allocs**), so the builtin's
  avoidance of the envelope is a genuine saving.
- `BenchmarkVerbTypedDispatchFork` (**0.98 ns/op, 0 allocs**) vs `BenchmarkVerbEnvelopeMarshal`
  (**1422 ns/op, 320 B, 6 allocs**) quantify the tax: the in-proc hot path is free; the wire envelope costs
  ~1.4µs/op, paid only out-of-process. **Go confirmed — the maximal-out-of-tree placement is viable.**

Test-only change (test files do not enter the binary, so no bed exercises it); the gate is the full
`go test ./...` + `go test -bench`, all green.

A pointer-bump cutover integrating the portaudio cleanup the spice dep-shed surfaced. Now that opus/portaudio
left core (the SPICE audio cgo code moved to candy/plugin-spice, gated behind `-tags spice_audio`) and the core
charly is built cgo-free (`ldd` shows no libportaudio/libopus): `box/arch` drops the redundant `portaudio`/
`opusfile` from the arch VM cloud_init + the false "exits 127 without libportaudio" comment (R10'd on
check-arch-vm, 60/60); `pkg/arch` drops the two now-false `-tags spice_audio` PKGBUILD optdepends (+ syncs
.SRCINFO); the `/charly-check:libvirt` + `/charly-vm:arch` skills are swept to the cgo-free reality (R5
claim-keyed). No core `charly/` change — this superproject commit bumps the box/arch + pkg/arch + plugins
submodule pointers.

### 2026-06-23 — feat(charly)!: Phase 4 dep-shed — externalize the `spice` verb; DROP Shells-com/spice + opus + portaudio from core

The fourth dependency-shedding cutover. The `spice` SPICE-wire check verb leaves the core for the new
out-of-process plugin `candy/plugin-spice/`, so charly's core `go.mod` **drops `github.com/Shells-com/spice`
+ `github.com/hraban/opus` + `github.com/gordonklaus/portaudio`** (the SPICE wire client + its cgo audio
codec transitives). `spice:` authoring is unchanged — the verb keeps its `spice:` discriminator +
`#SpiceMethod` enum + every modifier on the closed core `#Op` (it only leaves `#OpVerb`/`OpVerbs`/
`LiveVerbMethods`/`VerbCatalog`), dispatching via the registry → `invokeVerbProvider` over gRPC.

- `candy/plugin-spice/` (new external module): `provider.go` + `methods.go` + `session.go` port spice.go +
  spice_session.go's 7 methods (status/screenshot/cursor/click/mouse/type/key); the vendored
  `third_party/spice` (SPICE wire stack) moved here via `git mv` (its `//go:build spice_audio`-gated
  ch-playback/ch-record keep opus/portaudio OFF by default, so the plugin — like the old core — builds
  cgo-free). `charly/spice.go`, `spice_session.go`, `plugin_verb_spice.go` DELETED.
- **The host pre-resolves the SPICE endpoint:** `charly/vm_target.go` stays in core (`ResolveVmTarget` +
  `SpiceEndpoint` use go-libvirt + libvirtxml, shared with the VM machinery). `charly/spice_preresolve.go`
  adds `preresolveSpiceEndpoint` (wired into `invokeVerbProvider`): resolves the bed's VM → live SPICE
  endpoint host-side (opening the remote `qemu+ssh://` tunnel where needed), and passes the dialable
  address + password to the plugin via the env — so the plugin needs no go-libvirt, only Shells-com/spice.
- **New enabler (R3, general): a deploy's `add_candy` plugins now load.** The project candy scan
  (`CollectRemoteRefs`) only walks image-closure refs, so an `add_candy` plugin candy (spice has no domain
  candy in the bed's image closure, unlike adb/kube) was never fetched/loaded. `ResolveOpts.ExtraCandyRefs`
  (config.go/refs.go — additive, default-empty) routes the deploy's `add_candy` refs through the SAME
  collection primitive; `attachCheckRunnerContext` (the ONE shared check-runner plugin-load site) +
  `bundle_add_cmd.go` pass `deployAddCandyRefs(dir, name)` so a deploy loads ALL its composed plugins.
- No host `charly check spice` CLI — declarative verb only (mirrors adb/kube/appium). Skills (spice / check /
  libvirt / arch / ssh) + README swept to the verb-only framing (R5 claim-keyed); the stale `check_cmd.go:60`
  comment + the go-skill source-map (listing spice/k8s as in-core sub-Cmds) corrected.
- **Composition (cross-repo):** `box/arch` check-arch-vm bed `add_candy`s `plugin-spice`; `box/cachyos`
  `cachyos-gpu-desktop-check` candy `require:`s it (in the GPU image closure) — so both repos' `spice:`
  checks keep working (R2). The box `@github` pins for plugin-spice point at this cutover's tag.

R10: `go test ./...` + `task build:charly` + `charly box validate` (exit 0) + `grep Shells-com/spice|opus|
portaudio charly/go.mod` = 0 + the live `check-arch-vm` bed (a disposable libvirt Arch cloud VM with a SPICE
socket; plugin-spice host-built + served out-of-process over go-plugin gRPC, loaded via the add_candy enabler;
the verb speaking the SPICE wire — Main/Display/Inputs/Cursor channel enumeration — to the live VM; `spice:
status` → "SPICE: ok", `spice: screenshot` → a real 1280x800 native-SPICE-decode PNG) through a fresh `charly
update`: **60 passed / 0 failed** on BOTH check-live and the fresh-rebuild check-live.

### 2026-06-23 — feat(charly)!: Phase 4 dep-shed — externalize the `kube` verb + the k3s kubeconfig-merge + k8s status; DROP k8s.io/client-go + k8s.io/apimachinery from core

The third dependency-shedding cutover, and the largest client-go surface yet. The `kube` Kubernetes
cluster-probe verb, the k3s post-provision kubeconfig-merge, and the `charly status` k8s live-readiness probe
all leave the core for the new out-of-process plugin `candy/plugin-kube/`, so charly's core `go.mod` **drops
`k8s.io/client-go` + `k8s.io/apimachinery`** (and ~7 `k8s.io/*` / `sigs.k8s.io/*` transitives). `kube:`
authoring is unchanged — the verb keeps its `kube:` discriminator + `#KubeMethod` + every modifier on the
closed core `#Op` (it only leaves `#OpVerb`/`OpVerbs`/`LiveVerbMethods`/`VerbCatalog`), dispatching via the
registry → `invokeVerbProvider` over gRPC.

- `candy/plugin-kube/` (new external Go module): `provider.go` + `cluster.go` + `methods.go` port `k8s_cmd.go`'s
  13-method surface (nodes/wait-nodes/pods/wait-ready/ingress/ingressclass/storageclass/service/lb-external-ip/
  addons/apply/delete/raw) + the dynamic client; `merge.go` holds the kubeconfig merge. `charly/k8s_cmd.go`
  (944 lines) is DELETED.
- **Cluster pre-resolution stays in core (client-go-free):** `charly/k8s_config.go`'s `findK8sSpec` resolves a
  `cluster:` profile → kubeconfig context HOST-side (`preresolveKubeCluster`, wired into `invokeVerbProvider`)
  before marshaling, so the plugin receives a concrete kubeconfig+context and needs no ClusterProfile knowledge.
- **The k3s kubeconfig-merge re-homed:** `charly/k8s_plugin.go` adds `invokeKubePlugin`; `k3s_post.go`'s
  `mergeKubeconfig` now calls the plugin's `merge-kubeconfig` method (an internal deploy seam, not in the
  `#KubeMethod` enum). `K3sPostProvision` runs inside `charly bundle add`, which loads the deploy's composed
  plugins — so `candy/k3s-server` now `require:`s `plugin-kube`.
- **`charly status --nested` for kind:k8s deploys** now reports tree-state only (the client-go live-readiness
  probe in `status_collect_k8s.go` was dropped — live k8s health is asserted via a `kube:` check instead).
- There is no host `charly check kube` CLI subcommand — kube is a declarative check verb only (mirrors
  adb/appium). The `/charly-kubernetes:check-k8s`, `/charly-kubernetes:kubernetes`, k3s-server/k3s-agent,
  `/charly-check:check` skills, `CLAUDE.md`, `README.md`, and `candy/k8s-layer` were swept to the verb-only
  framing (R5 claim-keyed); the stale `LoadClusterProfile` reference (removed in schema v4) was corrected to
  `findK8sSpec`.
- **R1 — two bugs caught by R10, fixed in-tree:** (1) the VM check path (`runVm`) never loaded external plugins
  (kube was a builtin before, so it never needed to), making a VM bed's `kube:` steps SKIP as `unknown verb` —
  `runVm` now calls the shared `attachCheckRunnerContext` (the helper whose own contract says every RunModeLive
  baked-plan runner MUST call it, R3). (2) the bed's `kv-k8s-raw-version` check was DEGENERATE — it set a
  `text:` the raw method ignored and passed only because the original `raw`'s `required:["Resource"]` was a
  latent *unenforced* check; the plugin correctly enforces it, so the check was rewritten to a meaningful
  `kube_resource: namespaces` test asserting `kube-system`.

R10: `go test ./...` + `task build:charly` + `charly box validate` (exit 0) + `grep k8s.io|sigs.k8s
charly/go.mod` = 0 + the live `check-k3s-vm` bed (a disposable libvirt Arch VM + a real k3s control plane;
plugin-kube host-built + served out-of-process over go-plugin gRPC; the kubeconfig-merge via `invokeKubePlugin`
registering the cluster; all 13 kube methods probing the live cluster via `cluster: vm-k3s-vm`) through a fresh
`charly update`: **22 passed / 0 failed** on check-live against the freshly-built VM, the fresh-update rebuild

methods) + vnc (8) are the lowest-risk pair (TCP-only, stdlib) and prove the pattern.

`registerDedicatedBuiltin` path (the same mechanism the deploy/step/builder providers + deploy-shape kinds
use) — the FIRST live-container verbs to do so. It's a pure DISPATCH RELOCATION, not a schema change.

### 2026-06-23 — refactor(charly): Phase 2 deploy-shape — extract group/pod/vm/k8s/local/android into dedicated KindProviders

The hardest heavy-kind batch: the 6 deploy-shape kinds leave the core `kind_builtins.go` (which now hosts
ONLY `candy`) for dedicated builtin `KindProvider`s. **Design resolved by the code (RDD-proved on `group`
first):** unlike the tier-1 leaf kinds (distro/builder/…), these CANNOT use the JSON Invoke envelope —
they recurse over the `genericNode` member tree (pod members, vm→k8s nesting, resource siblings) and land
in the TYPED core maps (`uf.Bundle`/`uf.Pod`/`uf.VM`/`uf.K8s`/`uf.Local`/`uf.Android`) every deploy/check
consumer reads, neither of which survives serialization. So they stay **in-proc `KindProvider`s with typed
`DecodeNode`**, registered via `registerDedicatedBuiltin`, and the recursion helpers (`buildBundleNodeInto`,
`buildStandaloneResource`, `buildBundleNode`, `resourceChildren`) **stay in CORE** (byte-identical, only
relocated). External out-of-proc is correctly deferred to the ExecutorService enabler — placement stays a
build choice.

- `plugin_group.go` (groupKind) + `plugin_substrate.go` (the parameterized `standaloneKind{word,def}` +
  `isDeployShape`, with 5 thin `registerDedicatedBuiltin` registrations for pod/vm/k8s/local/android).
  Removed group/standalone/isDeployShape from `kind_builtins.go`, the 6 from `builtinProviderInstances`,
  and the 6 words from the `charly.yml` `providers:` manifest (now `kind: [candy]`).
- **Code-only — NO schema bump** (the authored keywords + core `#Pod`/`#Vm`/… defs are unchanged; HEAD
  stays `2026.174.1100`, no box re-stamp — superproject-only). `checkKindProviderBijection` still proves
  each is registered.

### 2026-06-23 — refactor(charly): Phase 2 tier-1 — extract distro/builder/init/resource/target into KindProvider plugins

The first heavy-kind batch: the 5 build-vocabulary / cross-ref kinds leave the core `kind_builtins.go`
typed `DecodeNode` for dedicated `KindProvider` plugin units, mirroring the clean-tier precedent
(agent/module/sidecar/package-group). **Code-only — NO schema bump:** extracting a kind leaves the
authored keyword (`distro:`/`builder:`/…) unchanged (the plugin decodes it), so it's a CUE-internal vocab
change (`#Node` arms / `KindWords`), not an authored wire-key change — no `MigrationStep`, HEAD stays
`2026.174.1100`, no box re-stamp (this is a superproject-only cutover).

- Per kind: `charly/plugin/builtins/<kind>/` (self-contained `#<Kind>Input` + plugin.go + params) +
  `plugin_<kind>.go` (`KindProvider`, Invoke→OpLoad → decode into the core `spec.<Kind>` → land in
  `uf.PluginKinds["<kind>"]`). The core `#<Kind>` defs stay in `schema/` (still generate the `spec.<Kind>`
  consumer types — zero consumer-type churn). Removed the 5 typed `*Kind` structs, the 5 `cue_kind_*.go`
  registrations, the `UnifiedFile.{Distro,Builder,Init,Resource,Target}` fields, the 5 `mergeXMap`
  funcs (subsumed by `mergePluginKindsMap`), and the manifest entries.
- Consumer rerouting (the real work): `Distros()`/`Builders()`/`Inits()`/`Resources()` accessors (a shared
  `decodePluginKindMap[T]` over `uf.PluginKinds`) replace every typed-field reader — the generator's
  `Project{Distro,Builder,Init}Config`, preempt/vm GPU arbitration, the migrate default-vocab compare.
  `target` has zero core readers (Calamares importers deferred) → no accessor (dead code, R5); its body
  rests in `PluginKinds["target"]`.
- **RCA fix (R1):** `distro` is BOTH a plugin kind AND a candy package-surface data key; `classifyDisc`
  checked `dataKeySet` before the plugin `ResolveKind`, mis-classing a top-level `distro:` node as `"data"`
  (dropping the non-deployable-kind child gate). Fixed: a registered plugin KIND now wins over a homonymous
  data key for a TOP-LEVEL node (the `asChild` data-sense path unchanged); only `distro` collides.

R10: `go test ./...` (charly + spec + the reserved-word bijection gates + CUE corpus/closedness) + `task
build:charly` + `charly box validate` exit 0 (root + box/fedora) + `charly box generate` (gen=0, proving
the box build reads distro/builder/init vocab through the new accessors) + check-pod.

### 2026-06-23 — feat(charly)!: extract the `file` verb — the LAST verb leaves `#Op` + schema HEAD → 2026.174.1100

The final verb extraction — **every check/state-provision verb is now a plugin** (`#OpVerb` is empty of
the legacy probe/act verbs). `file` is a shell-act state-provision verb (RDD corrected an initial
mis-scoping as pure-check): `fileVerb.RenderProvisionScript` is a RUNTIME file-creation act (touch+chmod),
distinct from the BUILD-time COPY of `write:`/`copy:`, so it's preserved — `fileVerb` implements
`CheckVerbProvider` (RunVerb → runFile) AND `ProvisionActor`, mirroring unix_group/user/mount/kernel-param.

- **Shared-field discipline:** `mode` is read by copy/write at deploy (`deploy_target_{local,vm}.go`), so
  it STAYS on `#Op` and is reproduced in `#FileInput` (the gid-between-unix_group-and-user pattern). Only
  the 7 file-exclusive fields (`file`/`exists`/`owner`/`group_of`/`filetype`/`contains`/`sha256`) leave `#Op`.
- **Third silent-regression caught (R5):** `contains` carries a bare-scalar **contains-default** (6 live
  candies rely on it — qemu-guest-agent, docker-ce, waybar-labwc, …); the generic `decodeMatcherList`
  (equals-default) would have silently flipped them to exact-equality. Added a dedicated `decodeContainsList`
  codec to preserve the semantic, and — `file` being its last user — fully removed the orphaned base
  `#ContainsList`/`ContainsList`/`expandContainsListNode` (CUE def, spec type, normalizer, tests + the stale
  refs in the `matching` plugin schema). `git grep '#ContainsList'` over `charly/` is clean.

The state-provision MigrationStep extended with file (check: AND run:); `calver-schema` + `LatestSchema
Version` `2026.174.0900` → `2026.174.1100`; cascaded across all 6 repos (B7); 181 main candies migrated.
(No @github version-adoption needed; all 5 boxes' standalone validate stayed exit 0.)

R10: `go test ./...` (incl. `TestRunner_FileVerb` + its bare-scalar-contains subtest, `TestDecodeContains
List`, the migrator check+run file cases, `TestEmitTasks_PluginAct_File` proving the migrated `plugin:
file` renders with zero "unknown verb" via the REAL box-build emit path, `TestCollectDescriptions_Bakes
PluginFileCheck`) + `task build:charly` + `charly box validate` exit 0 (root + all 5 boxes standalone) +
check-pod, whose check-live runs the migrated `plugin: file` checks.

### 2026-06-23 — feat(charly)!: extract the `package` verb (reuses TypedStepProvider) + retire the dead `LowersTo` field + schema HEAD → 2026.174.0900

The second typed-step state-provision verb, reusing the `TypedStepProvider` seam landed with `service`.
`package`'s run-act lowers to a TYPED `SystemPackagesStep` with reversals (`ReverseOpPackageRemove` +
`ReverseOpCoprDisable`) that the generic OpStep path would drop.

**package extracted:** `packageVerb` implements `CheckVerbProvider` (RunVerb → `runPackage`),
`TypedStepProvider` (LowersTo=`StepKindSystemPackages`; ConstructStep → `SystemPackagesStep{Format,
Phase, Packages}`), and `ProvisionActor`. **RDD:** `package`/`installed`/`version`/`package_map` are
package-exclusive (→ `#PackageInput`), but `exclude_distro` is SHARED — `runOne` reads it as a
per-verb skip-filter — so it STAYS on `#Op`. `resolvePackageName` (the distro-aware name resolver) stays
shared. The dead `case StepKindSystemPackages` in compileActOp (read the removed `Op.Package`) is deleted.

**R5 completion the extraction enables:** `package`/`service` were the ONLY `VerbSpec.LowersTo` users, and
service's lowering already moved into its provider — so `LowersTo` is now fully dead. Removed the struct
field, the 4th positional on every `VerbCatalog` entry, and simplified `ActsInBuildDeploy` to
`installVerbs[verb]`. Removed `package` from `#Op`/`VerbCatalog`/`spec.OpVerbs`/`builtinProviderInstances`/
the manifest.

The state-provision MigrationStep extended with package; `calver-schema` + `LatestSchemaVersion`
`2026.174.0700` → `2026.174.0900`; cascaded across all 6 repos (B7); 84 main candies migrated. (No @github
version-adoption needed — a pure migration the remote-cache auto-migration handles; all 5 boxes' standalone
validate stayed exit 0.)

R10: `go test ./...` (incl. the reversal-preservation gate — `plugin: package` compiles to a
`*SystemPackagesStep` whose `Reverse()` yields `ReverseOpPackageRemove` (+ `ReverseOpCoprDisable` for a
copr step), NOT an OpStep — + the act-emit test + the migrator test) + `task build:charly` + `charly box

### 2026-06-23 — feat(charly)!: TypedStepProvider enabler + extract the `service` verb + schema HEAD → 2026.174.0700

The typed-step-outlier state-provision verb. `service`'s run-act lowers to a TYPED `ServicePackagedStep`
with load-bearing reversals (`ReverseOpServiceDisable`/`RestoreEnabled`/`RemoveDropin`) that the
generic OpStep + `RenderProvisionScript` path would silently DROP.

**The TypedStepProvider enabler:** a new `TypedStepProvider` interface (`Provider` + `LowersTo() Step
Kind` + `ConstructStep(op, layer, img) InstallStep`). `compileActOp`, for a `plugin` verb, resolves the
provider and — if it's a `TypedStepProvider` — `return`s `ConstructStep(...)` (the typed step, whose
`Reverse()` then auto-records the reverse-ops exactly as before), falling through to the generic OpStep
only for pure-check / RenderProvisionScript plugins (command/etc.). The dead `case StepKindService
Packaged` in compileActOp (which read the now-removed `Op.Service`) is deleted (R5).

**service extracted:** `serviceVerb` implements ALL THREE — `CheckVerbProvider` (RunVerb → `runService`),
`TypedStepProvider` (LowersTo + ConstructStep → `ServicePackagedStep`), and `ProvisionActor`
(RenderProvisionScript, the runtime/opt-in live-act path). **RDD correction:** `running`/`enabled` had
ZERO remaining `#Op` readers after extraction (process reads its OWN `plugin_input.running`), so all of
`service`/`running`/`enabled` moved into `#ServiceInput` and left `#Op` — and the stale "running STAYS
in #Op" claim in `process.cue` was swept (R1 doc-divergence). Removed `service` from `#Op`/`VerbCatalog`
(its `LowersTo` now lives in the provider)/`spec.OpVerbs`/`builtinProviderInstances`/the manifest.

The state-provision MigrationStep extended with service (check: AND run:); `calver-schema` + `Latest
SchemaVersion` `2026.174.0500` → `2026.174.0700`; cascaded across all 6 repos (B7); 40 main candies
migrated. (No @github version-adoption needed — service is a pure migration the remote-cache
auto-migration handles; all 5 boxes' standalone validate stayed exit 0.)

R10: `go test ./...` (incl. the **reversal-preservation gate** — `plugin: service` compiles to a
`*ServicePackagedStep` whose `Reverse()` yields all 3 reverse-ops, NOT an OpStep — + the act-emit test +
the migrator test) + `task build:charly` + `charly box validate` exit 0 (root + all 5 boxes standalone)
+ check-pod — whose `check-stack-layer` candy's `plugin: service` enables `check-sleep` via the typed

### 2026-06-23 — feat(charly)!: extract the `command` verb into a plugin unit (the install-task act seam) + schema HEAD → 2026.174.0500

The hardest state-provision-tier verb. `command` is dual-natured but UNLIKE the RenderProvisionScript
verbs: its run-act is the full `emitCmd` path (the `bash <<'OVCMD'` heredoc, cache mounts, from_host
bind-mounts, BUILD_ARCH) — un-expressible as a provision-script string. So it's install-task-like, not
state-provision-like.

- **Check side:** `commandVerb` is a CheckVerbProvider (`plugin_verb_command.go` — named to avoid the
  CLI `plugin_command_*.go` files); RunVerb decodes `plugin_input` → `params.CommandInput`, reads the
  matchers from the step Op.
- **Act side (Option A):** `emitTasks` (`case "plugin"`) + `renderOpCommand` get a localized `if t.Plugin
  == "command"` branch that rehydrates `Op{Command,…}` from `plugin_input` and falls into the existing
  `emitCmd` — ONE shared command emitter, no duplication.
- **RDD correction:** `command` is a SHARED `#Op` modifier — `wl`/`libvirt` read `Op.Command` as their
  argv — so `command` STAYS in `#Op`, leaving only the `#OpVerb` union. Only `background`/`from_host`/
  `in_container` are command-exclusive (→ `#CommandInput`); the matchers `stdout`/`stderr`/`exit_status`
  stay shared in `#Op`. The MigrationStep field-SPLITS accordingly (exclusive fields → plugin_input,
  matchers stay at step level), gated by `stepHasCharlyVerb` so a `wl`/`libvirt`+command step is not
  converted.

**Validation restoration (R2, surfaced + fixed):** `collectCheckRefs` now scans `plugin_input` —
RESTORING the `${VAR}`-in-build-scope check that the earlier http extraction silently dropped when
fields moved off `#Op`. It surfaced 4 pre-existing latent bugs (build-scope steps referencing the
runtime `${HOST_PORT}`): `candy/testapi` steps 4/5 and `candy/{kde-selkies,selkies-kde-desktop}` — all
fixed by adding `context: [runtime]`.

`calver-schema` + `LatestSchemaVersion` `2026.174.0300` → `2026.174.0500`; cascaded across all 6 repos
(B7); 144 main candies + the box candies migrated.

**Cross-repo note (B7 step 5):** box/cachyos + box/fedora pin the selkies/testapi candies via `@github`
at `v2026.170.1105` (a deliberate lag). The restored check correctly flags the scope bug in those
FROZEN pinned copies — fixed at the producer's (main) HEAD here; the consumers' standalone validate
clears when those pins adopt the fix in the immediate-next version-adoption cutover. The cutover's R10
(check-pod, assembled with the local-main override) and the boxes' assembled-context validate both pass.

R10: `go test ./...` (incl. `TestEmitTasks_PluginAct…` + the command field-split migrator test) + `task
build:charly` + `charly box validate` exit 0 (root + the assembled box context) + check-pod — whose
composed candies exercise migrated `plugin: command` check AND run-act steps, the act emitting a real
`RUN` block (verified: `unknown verb "command"`/`"plugin"` count = 0 in the generated Containerfile).

### 2026-06-23 — feat(charly)!: extract 3 shared-path state-provision verbs (user/mount/kernel-param) + schema HEAD → 2026.174.0300

The state-provision batch on the proven act-emit enabler: `user`, `mount`, `kernel-param` each leave
the closed `#Op` into dedicated builtin plugin units that are BOTH a `CheckVerbProvider` (RunVerb →
`runUser`/`runMount`/`runKernelParam`) AND a `ProvisionActor` (RenderProvisionScript). Each verb's
fields move into its `#<Verb>Input`:

- **user** owns `user`/`uid`/`gid`/`home`/`shell` — and a confirmed handoff: `gid`/`uid` were held in
  `#Op` only because `runUser` read them; now that `user` leaves, NO other `#Op` verb reads them, so
  they're removed from `#Op` (unix_group's `#UnixGroupInput` already reproduces `gid` standalone).
- **mount** owns `mount`/`mount_source`/`filesystem`/`opt` (`opt` a `MatcherList`).
- **kernel-param** — kept the hyphenated wire word (a clean EXTRACTION, not a rename; the Go package
  dir is `kernel_param` only because hyphens are illegal in Go identifiers).

**R10-caught fix (R2/R4):** the `kernel-param` CHECK shelled to `sysctl`, absent in the minimal check-pod
image (exit 127). Hardened `runKernelParam` to read `/proc/sys/<dotted-key-as-slash-path>` directly via
`cat` inside the target (kernel params are netns-scoped — the target's `/proc/sys` is the source of
truth) — `sysctl -n k` ≡ `/proc/sys/k`, so the value is identical with ZERO external dependency. The
`run:` ACT keeps `sysctl -w` (a deploy/runtime context). The value `MatcherList` is preserved.

**Surfaced + flagged (R2, separable → its own follow-up):** the `groups` field in `#Op` is now DEAD
(no runtime reader — orphaned by the unix_group cutover whose `#UnixGroupInput` reproduced only
`unix_group`+`gid`). Left in `#Op`, annotated, for an immediate-next cleanup cutover.

The MigrationStep `state-provision-verbs-to-plugin` extended with the 3 verbs (BOTH check: AND run:).
`calver-schema` + `LatestSchemaVersion` `2026.174.0100` → `2026.174.0300`; cascaded across all 6 repos
(B7).

R10: `go test ./...` (incl. per-verb emit-path tests + `TestRunner_KernelParam` reading `/proc/sys` +
the migration test) + `task build:charly` + `charly box validate` exit 0 across all 6 repos (every
root at `2026.174.0300`) + check-pod — `check-user-present` (root via getent), `check-mount-present`
(/proc via findmnt), `check-kernel-param-readable` (/proc/sys/kernel/ostype = Linux), all live. 5
submodule pointers bumped.

### 2026-06-23 — feat(charly)!: act-emit enabler for state-provision verbs + extract unix_group + schema HEAD → 2026.174.0100

Opens the STATE-PROVISION verb tier (verbs that are BOTH a check-probe AND a run-act that lowers to an
install-plan step). The enabler is the act-side analogue of the runPluginVerb check enabler.

**The act-emit enabler (the missing half):** a state-provision verb's runtime act (`ProvisionActor.
RenderProvisionScript`) was already plugin-ready, but the install-plan EMIT paths
(`compileActOp`/`renderOpCommand`/`emitTasks`) switched on `Op.File`/`Op.Command`/… with no Plugin
case — so a `run: {plugin: <verb>}` step would break ("task has no supported verb"). Added ONE shared
helper `resolveProvisionScript(op, distros)` that resolves `op.Plugin` → type-asserts `ProvisionActor`
→ calls `RenderProvisionScript`, wired into all THREE emit sites: the box/OCI build's candy-walk
emitter `emitTasks` (the path `charly box generate`→`writeCandySteps` actually uses), the local/vm
deploy `renderOpCommand`, and the runtime `runProvisionAct` (which would also have broken, R2). `OpStep`
gained a `Distros` field for the context. A non-`ProvisionActor` plugin in a `run:` step errors loudly
(R4). This one seam serves all 6 shared-path state-provision verbs. (R10 caught a first attempt that
wired the OCI seam into `OCITarget.emitOp` — used only for pod-overlay rendering, NOT the base image
build — which a unit test masked but the check-pod bed exposed as `# unknown verb "plugin" — skipping`;
the fix moved the single seam into `emitTasks`, the emitter both the box build AND the pod overlay
share, and deleted the divergent `emitOp` pre-conversion, R5.)

**unix_group extracted** (the cleanest first — build-safe `groupadd`, no reversals): its `unixGroup
Verb` is registered as a plugin unit that is BOTH a `CheckVerbProvider` (RunVerb → `runUnixGroup`) AND
a `ProvisionActor` (RenderProvisionScript → groupadd). **Key catch:** `gid` is SHARED (`runUser` reads
`Op.GID`), so `gid` stays in `#Op`; `#UnixGroupInput` reproduces it standalone. Removed the
`unix_group` discriminator from `#Op`/`VerbCatalog`/`spec.OpVerbs`/`builtinProviderInstances`/the
manifest.

A dedicated MigrationStep `state-provision-verbs-to-plugin` (@ `2026.174.0050`) converts BOTH a
`check:` AND a `run:` step's `unix_group:` → `plugin: unix_group` (the goss migrator only handled
`check:` — wrong for a dual-natured verb). `calver-schema` + `LatestSchemaVersion` `2026.173.2300` →
`2026.174.0100`; cascaded across all 6 repos (B7).

R10: `go test ./...` (incl. `TestRenderOpCommand_PluginAct_UnixGroup` (local/vm), `TestEmitOp_Plugin
Act_UnixGroup_OCI` (build), `…NotActCapable` (the loud error), + the migration test) + `task build:
charly` + `charly box validate` exit 0 across all 6 repos (every root at `2026.174.0100`) + check-pod —
whose composed `check-stack-layer` candy emits the `run: plugin: unix_group` **groupadd at image
build** (the act-emit enabler end-to-end), then the `check: plugin: unix_group` step verifies the group
exists at runtime. 5 submodule pointers bumped.

### 2026-06-23 — feat(charly)!: externalize the observe verbs http/interface/addr into plugin units + schema HEAD → 2026.173.2300

Observe-verb wave 2 (after process/port/dns): `http`, `interface`, `addr` leave the closed `#Op`/
`spec.OpVerbs` into dedicated builtin plugin units (`plugin: <verb>` + `plugin_input`), reusing their
existing `runHTTP`/`runInterface`/`runAddr` impls. `http`'s `body`/`header` matchers ride the shared
`MatcherList` JSON codec (R3), the matching pattern.

**RDD refinements:** (1) `method`/`request_body` (shared with cdp/dbus/libvirt) + `timeout` (a general
per-step modifier read by `probeNeverHang`) STAY in `#Op` — only http-exclusive fields leave. (2) R5
orphan cleanup: once `interface`/`addr` leave, `addrs` (dns already extracted) and `reachable` (port
already extracted) have no remaining `#Op` consumer — both removed from `#Op`.

**R2/R3 latent-bug fix (surfaced + fixed in-scope):** `opExpandVars`/`collectHostRefs` only walked
`#Op` `StringFields`, so `${HOST_PORT:N}`/`${VAR}`/`${HOST:member}` inside a migrated step's
`plugin_input` was never expanded — a latent break for the already-landed process/port/dns too (all 32
corpus `addr` uses are `127.0.0.1:${HOST_PORT:N}`). Added generic `plugin_input` walks
(`expandAnyVars`/`collectAnyStrings`) — fixes http/addr AND retroactively repairs process/port/dns.
Also rewired `k8s_generate.checkToProbe` + the result-subject label to read the discriminator from
`plugin_input` via a generic `pluginInputStr` helper (else K8s httpGet/tcpSocket probes + report
subjects vanished for migrated steps).

**`command` recategorized (RDD, NOT scope-narrowing):** `command` is dual-natured — `check: command:`
is a probe BUT `run: command:` lowers via `compileActOp` to a generic `OpStep` emitted as a
Containerfile `RUN` (`emitCmd`), so removing `Op.Command` from `#Op` breaks the build exactly like
package/service. It is a STATE-PROVISION verb (420 corpus uses, ~97 act steps) — extracted later with
file/package/service via the check-verb + step-provider composition, not here.

One generalized MigrationStep `goss-verbs-to-plugin` (extended `gossVerbFields` with http/interface/
addr); `calver-schema` + `LatestSchemaVersion` `2026.173.1742` → `2026.173.2300`; cascaded across all
6 repos (B7). 38 main-repo candy manifests migrated (RDD-proven on a temp copy first).

R10: `go test ./...` (incl. the extended `TestMigrateGossVerbsToPlugin_SecondWave` + the rewired
k8s-probe/host-ref/report tests + the full corpus test) + `task build:charly` + `charly box validate`
exit 0 across all 6 repos (every root at `2026.173.2300`) + check-pod (migrated `plugin: http`/`addr`
via check-stack-layer + the new `plugin: interface` step + the `${HOST_PORT}` resolution, live). 5
submodule pointers bumped.

### 2026-06-23 — feat(charly): externalize the `sidecar` kind into a plugin unit (Phase 2 — Cutover B2; clean-tier kinds complete)

The last clean-tier kind, and the payoff for the name-keyed override enabler. `sidecar` leaves the
closed core into a dedicated builtin plugin unit (`charly/plugin/builtins/sidecar/` +
`plugin_sidecar.go`). The `uf.Sidecar` reader audit confirmed the simplification: the ~15 deploy
consumers read the PROJECTED `Config.Sidecar`/`BundleConfig.Sidecar` fields (or resolved
`[]ResolvedSidecar`, or command flags) — NOT `uf.Sidecar`. The only direct readers were the 2
projections + the doc/embed merges + one extra deploy-time site (`EmbeddedSidecarTemplates()`), all
rewired to a new `func (uf *UnifiedFile) Sidecars() map[string]SidecarDef` accessor.

**The overridable embedded tailscale — Cutover A's reason to exist:** the embedded `tailscale` sidecar
is an authored `sidecar:` node in `charly/charly.yml`, so it now loads through the plugin path
(`runPluginKind` → `#SidecarInput`) on every `LoadUnified`. The explicit `mergeSidecarMap` in
`applyEmbeddedDefaults` is DELETED — replaced by the generic name-keyed root-wins
`mergePluginKindsMap`. RDD-proven (`TestEmbeddedDefaults_SidecarProjectWins`): a project authoring
`sidecar: tailscale` with a custom image OVERRIDES the embedded one — root wins, one entry — and the
complex tailscale (cap_add + env + volume + secret) round-trips end-to-end through `#SidecarInput`.

`#Sidecar` stays in `schema/` for the canonical `spec.Sidecar`/`SidecarDef` (`cue_types_gen.go`
byte-identical — zero deploy-consumer type churn). Removed `sidecarKind`/`cue_kind_sidecar.go`/`uf.
Sidecar`/`mergeSidecarMap` + from `#Node`/`_reservedNode`/`builtinProviderInstances`/the `kind:`
manifest; `vocab_gen.go` drops `sidecar` from `KindWords`. **The clean-tier kinds (package-group,
module, agent, sidecar) are now all externalized.**

**MAIN-ONLY**: authoring (`sidecar:`) unchanged — no `#Node` version bump, no MigrationStep, no
cascade. `charly box validate` exit 0 at root AND box/fedora (both parse the embedded tailscale
through `#SidecarInput`).

R10: `go test ./...` (incl. the override test + the end-to-end embedded-tailscale resolve + the full
existing sidecar deploy/quadlet suite) + `task build:charly` + `charly box validate` exit 0 (root +
box/fedora) + check-pod (the embedded tailscale sidecar flows through the plugin path on the fresh
binary).

### 2026-06-22 — feat(charly): externalize the `module` + `agent` kinds into plugin units (Phase 2 — Cutover B1)

Built on the name-keyed plugin-kind enabler. Two kinds leave the closed core into dedicated builtin
plugin units (`charly/plugin/builtins/{module,agent}/` + `plugin_{module,agent}.go`):

- **`module`** (zero functional readers — clean, package-group-style): routed to `uf.PluginKinds
  ["module"]`; `uf.Module` + `mergeModuleMap` + the dead `ModuleSpec` alias removed (R5).
- **`agent`** (name-keyed, load-bearing consumers): the entity now lands in `uf.PluginKinds["agent"]`
  via the name-keyed mechanism; a new `func (uf *UnifiedFile) Agents() map[string]*AgentConfig`
  accessor decodes it back into the catalog, and EVERY reader is rewired to it — the 4 `ResolveAgent`
  sites + `PrintAgents` + the **load-bearing `validateIterateBed` guard** (an iterate bed naming an
  unknown agent must still hard-fail — proven by a dedicated test). `uf.Agent` + `mergeAgentMap`
  removed (R5).

**The `#Agent`/`#Module` defs stay in `schema/`** (generating the canonical `spec.Agent`/`spec.Module`
the plugins' `Invoke` decodes into, exactly as `#Group` stayed for package-group) — each plugin
carries a self-contained `#<Kind>Input` reproduction for validation. So `AgentConfig = spec.Agent`
survives and `spec/cue_types_gen.go` is untouched — zero consumer-type churn across the ~20 harness
sites. Removed from `#Node`/`_reservedNode`/`builtinProviderInstances`/the `kind:` manifest;
`vocab_gen.go` drops `agent`/`module` from `KindWords`.

**MAIN-ONLY**: authoring unchanged (`agent:`/`module:` stay) — no `#Node` version bump, no MigrationStep,
no cascade. `charly box validate` exit 0 at the unchanged `2026.173.1742` proves `#AgentInput` accepts
the 3 real `claude`/`codex`/`gemini` iterate nodes.

Agent` (the guard), `TestLoadUnified_ModulePluginKind`, + the rewritten plugin-load validation test) +
